<Review>I'll start this review with the good stuff. The lady who assisted me was great. While my overall experience at this location was not positive I could tell she was doing the best she could with a bad situation. I wish I remembered her name because she deserves a raise.

Now for the bad stuff. This location is only open till noon on Saturdays which causes a big back log of people needing to pick up up their rentals and also people needing to return their rentals. It took me an hour to get my car since they ran out of cars and were waiting for people to do returns so they could immediately give those cars out to at least a dozen people who were waiting in the small location office.

The staff did the best they could with the limited resources they had and they were able to deal with irritated customers in a professional manner.

My advice to the public would be to avoid renting from this location on a Saturday or if you have to make the reservation for Saturday, make it as early as possible in the day.

My advice to the management of this location would be to consider leaving the office open an extra few hours on Saturdays to prevent these sorts of backlogs.
